Hi Guys,

-DutchTrade is your specialist in MDMA!

Looking at the messages on the forum I guess it would be an honor if you guys compare us to Dutchaanbod, but please know that we're not them.
DutchTrade stands for:
- Fast delivery; orders will be sent within 24 hours after placing your order
- For orders >50 gram, we work with track&trace, for orders less than 50g we can provide track&trace on request and for an additional payment of US$5,00
- Good quality and prices
- Fast communication; messages will be answered within 24 hours
- Professional, secure and discrete packaging; all orders are vacuumed and packed in moisture barrier bags
- You don't need to finalize early!

TAKE ADVANTAGE OF OUR SPECIAL WELCOME OFFER:
-The first 100 orders (>5 gram) will get 10% extra.
-We offer free samples for customers in Germany but do request a (positive) review in return.

If you have any questions about our product, work method or else, please read our faq on our SR profile or send us a message
Best regards

DutchTrade crew

Just received my 10G from DUTCHTRADE.  Here's my review.

VENDOR: DutchTrade

PRODUCT: 10G MDMA Actual weight-12.23g

COMMUNICATION 5/5 Very polite, fast responses-easy to understand and straight to the point.

SHIPPING: 4/5 Ordered 2/15, shipped 2/18?, received 2/27 to upper midwest.  However, I am giving a 4/5 due to the single layer food grade vacuum seal and the fact that before opened, I could hear the product rattling within the stealth.  Once opened, I could smell the odor of the product through the sealed bag which means that a dog could easily pick up the scent within the package.

STEALTH: 5/5 On point with Dutchaanbod and Interways, which has still provided me with a 100% success rate for orders coming out of Germany (I have now used PF, Dutchaanbod, Afterhour, Interways and Dutchtrade)

PRODUCT ?/5  HOLY SHIT!  This shit looks and smells on point with Dutchaanbod, which if you had the opportunity to taste, you already know it's fire.  I rolled on Monday, after 3 months of not doing so, on Interways mediocre shit but I know I'll be testing this product out within the next couple days.  Bunch of chunks with crystal powder.

Overall, he is a stand up vendor.  I still have another 20g on the way from interways 'new batch' so I'll post a review on here about that product when it comes, which will probably be next week.  Either way, I think I have found my new bulk vendor with DutchTrade and am very pleased with the service that I received from him.

I'll post a picture when I get around to it.  Order from Dutch with confidence.

On a personal note-I know for a fact we have a very high quality vendor here and so far since I've been on the road (which will be a year in a couple weeks) I've seen several vendors who WERE good quality vendors get fucked in the ass by scammers getting their shit and still getting refunds.  I swear to god, I will be LIVID if this happens to DutchTrade.  So PLEASE, DO NOT FUCK THIS GUY OVER!!!!!!!  DON'T RUIN A GOOD THING  FOR ALL OF US AND FOR THE LOVE OF GOD FINALIZE YOUR ORDERS WHEN YOU RECEIVE THEM!

Summer is coming up, which is festival season, and I was caught in a shit frenzy last year with Pf and really don't want this to happen again!

Title: Re: DutchTrade
Post by: DeadRa7 on March 04, 2013, 04:24 am
Quote from: luckypunk11 on March 04, 2013, 02:25 am

anymore reviews/ trip reports guys?

Alright guys, sorry it took me so long to post my trip report: last night I went out again and fell into a k hole all night-but that's a different story for a different day. 

Friday night I went to a jam band style show-not my ideal setting but my girl loves that type of music and she comes to all my EDM shows so I said fuck it, maybe dutch's MDMA would make it more fun (it did, to a certain extent)

T-0:00 (10:20 PM) Dropped 200MG capped up of dutch's gear in the car before I went in-the 10 gram order I just received the previous day.  I rolled last Monday off Interways shit, which was fairly weak (hour roll tops) and before that it had been since November since I rolled, so I'd still consider my tolerance fairly low-although I have been consuming MDMA-type products for several years I know exactly what  to expect from a good, clean roll. Anyways, I was completely sober from other chemicals, alcohol and weed included, before I started rolling.

T-0:30 Small come up effects were noticed, although it was so fucking cold inside and out which made me feel quite uncomfortable. 

T-1:00 As I was dancing with my girl while the band was jamming out, I started to feel the full on effects of the drug come on.  It was very euphoric and my entire body felt amazing

T-1:30 Band goes on intermission so we have a seat and just start touching each other all over, enjoying the sensations from the simple rub of the back, arms and stomach.  We decide we want to be in bed together, so we left right there and drove an hour home (but it seemed like an eternity)

T-2:30 we each drop another 100MG upon returning home, laid on the couch and we're just kissing, touching eachother and got completely naked.  It was an amazing feeling-I'd honestly never rolled this hard around a girl (especially one I'm madly in love with) and her touch was orgasmic everywhere she touched.  Jaw was clenching (HARD!) and my pupils were the size of a motherfuckin' dime. 

T-2:40 The redose hit us like a brick wall to the point we could not stop talking, but were forgetting almost everything we were saying right after it was said (it was kinda funny, actually).  We just laid there, naked, talking about everything and anything that was on our minds.  Literally, my entire body and mind was in complete bliss to the point that I can't even put into words on here. 

T-4:00 We started to smoke some bowls of weed and each took a couple MG of xanax as the slow comedown started to occur. 

T-5:00 The roll was basically gone, however still laying with my girl was very euphoric in itself and we both gradually fell asleep a short time afterwards-woke up feeling like a million bucks.  Hah!  Take that alcohol! 

I know this might sound like a sappy love story, but seriously having her there made the experience one hell of a one.  It's almost like we fell back in love with each other.  I will be completely honest and say this is some very, very high quality product that will easily resale for $15-20 a tenth and at least $100 a gram at certain events across the country (you all better know what I'm referring to). 

DutchTrade is the new dutchaanbod IMO, I will be putting in a massive order next week based on my experience with this 10g transaction.  If anybody has any questions they'd like answered in particular, please don't hesitate to contact me or PM.

I'll say it once again though, DO NOT FUCK THIS GUY OVER!!!!!!  This is a very Honest vendor, amazing prices, fucking fire product and very decent stealth measures which will earn him his place in the top 1% within the next two months, and I just hope that he isn't a single man operation like PF was otherwise this will go to shit by late May-June.

I have already specified that I am located in the USA several times in this thread as I've kept others buyers updated. Track and Trace is REGISTERED MAIL and by USPS policy, requires a signature upon delivery/signing the slip they leave if you are not there. Few and far between you get postal workers who don't want to walk to your door or whatever so they leave it in the mailbox. This is the *exception*, not the rule. There really isn't much further discussion regarding that topic.

Regardless, if you are getting 100+ grams of MDMA to your door, and they find out, pretty sure you are gonna get nailed whether you scribble your name or not. The BEST way to prevent a conviction is to: 1. Do NOT have drugs in your house when waiting for a delivery. A little bud is one thing, but seriously..No drugs. This is way more important than any signature you could ever sign. 2. Encrypt your electronic footprint.

I don't know where the idea comes from that the police need a signature to secure any sort of conviction. That's just silly to even think about. I don't know specifics but considering how often people's doors get busted down incorrectly, I don't think it'd be too hard to talk a judge into serving a warrant upon discovery of a quarter-pound of marijuana coming to your home. Let me reiterate..A single signature is NOT your last defense in preventing arrest, nor is it ANY defense.

Title: Re: DutchTrade
Post by: BallsTripped on March 15, 2013, 07:42 pm
I understand the idea of taking as many precautions as possible, but I haven't seen a single bit of evidence from any source that using Tor to track your package will get it "flagged."  This is urban legend.

USPS has tens of thousands of tracking numbers going into their system every day and MILLIONS of people tracking their packages at the same time.  If you think they've set up an entire system to weed out and identify specific tracking numbers based on Tor usage, you're fucking high.  USPS barely has the resources to just maintain their basic services, and there's no fucking way they're wasting them on trying to differentiate contraband based on how the tracking is being accessed.  It would require a massive manpower effort with huge numbers of false positives and plucking individual packages out of the system based on a very low percentage of success.  They simply don't have the time or resources to even consider it, and that should be obvious if you think about it for half a second.

Believe all the paranoid fantasies you want, but unless you can point to some actual proof, then you need to identify your advice as "better safe than sorry" rather than something based on reality.

The only way your use of tracking could be used against you would be after the fact when you've been already been caught via a different means of identification.  And if that's the case, you're more than likely already fucked and the tracking would by no means be significant evidence one way or the other.

As you can see all over this thread DT has his shipping & communications down!!! And the price is nothing to complain about either!!

I just wonted to post a quick update about the quality of Dutchtrades Mdma, Im not posting a whole trip report because im lazy, but i do have experience with alot of different SR mdma vendors over the years .......

 The batch that I received looked brown/tan while sealed in the vacuum bag but after opening it and dosing out alot of capsules i notices its mostly white with a tan hue.. That being said it is still darker in color than any other mdma iv received off SR...  I tested the mdma when it first arrived and it passed marquis nicely (only test i had available at the moment)... After giving out some average dosed (150mg) to close friends that have SR mdma experience i was a little worried that the quality wouldn't compare to previous vendors...

SO this weekend i taste tested some myself...I only had one does of 150mg with 1000mg magnesium which is a good test point for me, and i will say that this is good strong mdma... 
-Started feeling first effects in average time (20-30min)..
-The come-up was very strong, (had me laying down in front of my home stereo speaker while my eyes were shuttering all over), but the come-up didnt seem to last very long (sry i cant be   more precise)...
-After the come-up i remember plateauing for a hour or so which was real nice but this is when i noticed a pretty strong jaw lock...It wasnt the worst iv had but it was pretty strong for only one dose...I also was having a hard time reading my phone or watching tv because my eyes were outta focus/shuttering..
-The ride down was smooth but had a small speedy/tweaky feeling to it...After a xanxa sleep was no issue..
- The next day i felt fine but i contribute that to only taking one dose and not redosing my serotonin away like iv been know to do...

Conclusion:
This is mdma and is very good mdma for the price..I felt it lacked in the empathy department and was a little speedier than iv grown accustom to lately, but would be good in a concert/club setting... I will be placing another order as soon as these kids get off spring break...lol...

2TheHaters:
It may sound like im trying to down grade DT's molly and this is not the case... SR has spoiled me sense iv been here with high quality mdma and i now feel like i can tell a difference in effects from different vendors or batches...And i am just trying to do my part in these forums with honesty..
 (Everyone locally loves it and its selling faster than bitcoins are fluctuating).......  Im only pointing out my experience with it and how it compares in quality to vendors from my past (dopeboy, PF, AF, SKY, Dutchaanbod, Etc....)

Title: Re: DutchTrade
Post by: spitroast on March 22, 2013, 02:25 pm
With much disappointment, I find myself finally joining the forums to post about a less than good experience.

My delivery strategy relies on not having to sign for a package. DT's profile explicitly stated that with the quantity I was ordering, no signature would be required. I'm also EU, so the problems that the Americans posting in this thread have had about signing for being added on shouldn't apply. The parcel eventually came, and the delivery man was not the regular one, and he was asking for a signature in the name sent to. This set off alarm bells, and I said that the recipient didn't live there any more. However, reading the thread, I'm now thinking that maybe this wasn't a controlled delivery, and that DT actually did send via registered postage. So I have now potentially rejected a normal delivery, on the basis of DT's shipping not being as advertised.

What should I do? I feel a little hard done-by taking a hit on this, I would expect a vendor to follow their advertised policy. In addition I have tried to contact them, the message has been read for quite a while but there hasn't been any reply. I feel it's unfair that I might have to choose between the two bad options of either finalising payment and receiving nothing, to protect my buyer statistics, or possibly accepting a 50% refund, which also doesn't look too great for me.

I'm posting to ask for advice on how to proceed, maybe prompt DT to respond to me (I've since filed a request to extend auto-finalization in the hope that they resend the package to me), but also just to make other buyers aware that DT don't seem to be following their advertised policy, and to take that into account when considering purchasing.

Until now I've had nothing but good experiences with other vendors on Silk Road, it's quite disheartening to be coming to the forums for the first time with this!

Thanks for your time.

No MBB, just the standard vac seal bag.

Big turn off. Dogs can smell through normal food grade PE-bags in a matter of hours. If you use normal bags, it's the same that you would just pack them in ziplock bags.

"VAC SEALING A BAGGIE OF ANYTHING IS NOT STEATH.

After 15 minutes of vac sealing, a PE vac sealed bag is vapour permeable, and detectable by sniffer dog.

F-i-f-t-e-e-n M-i-n-u-t-e-s.

Now I realise that vapour permeability is not the only important factor, but it's THE MOST IMPORTANT.  If a dog singles out a group of packages, the chances of you package being seized is 1000 times higher than it not."

Post by: XxWINxX94x23 on April 04, 2013, 03:16 am
Re-posting as a follow-up to my pack being received.

COMMUNICATION:
Not much needed, but vendor answered my questions in a timely manner.

TIME:
Took total of 17 days to the Land of Liberty, vendor marked in-transit on the correct day, according to the postage on the package. Did NOT require a signature with the "Worldwide" option. I believe the "Track & Trace" method requires a signature.

WEIGHT:
Ordered 20g + 10%, received 21.91g, which is a great fucking deal for how much I paid!

PRODUCT:
Product is about 60% chunks/rocks, 40% powder, with a few large rocks here and there. Has a clear/white consistency with a few darker patches and random off-color chunks.

TEST:
Don't have a Marquis/Mecke, but taste tested a little bit and its very bitter! Delightfully disgusting, just how good MDMA should be  8)

PACKAGING:
I'm going to be THAT guy who bitches about the packaging. I really think this method is over-used, it is nearly identical to Dutchaanbod's and ST's method, and could be improved by using MBB/Mylar bags and adding more layers. Nevertheless, it made it through and I can't claim it was seized for lack of protection.

COMMENTS:
DT is a great vendor, he actually ships when marked in-transit, and the product looks fire. Shipping was a little slow, but it made it! My only advice would be to personalize/add to the packaging a little bit. One of the best vendor's I've ever dealt with, highly recommend!

I agree MBB's should be used, but what you are saying is wrong.

I'm sorry :( I really don't mean to scare anyone away and I appreciate your input on this matter.

But yes, the 3m Dri-Shield is basically the same as welding the shipment inside a lump of steel. Absolutely no chance of smell if the sealing is done properly. IMHO all self-respectful vendors should step up the packaging the tiny bit up and standardize on foil, mylar or MBB (MBB being the best option). It basically renders the sniffer dogs useless. Making detection possible only by irregularities shown on possible x-ray or closer inspection (opening the letter, which is very uncommon and illegal in some parts of the world).

While DT's packaging method most likely is pretty ok. It can always be improved with a layer of MBB. It's only around a dollar more per shipment to apply that layer of "true stealth". DT could be the new number one MDMA German vendor if he just puts that tiny little investment into mastering the package. (the additional cost of MBB can be implemented into the shipping price)

My Source of info:
Testing made by Thisaintme
http://dkn255hz262ypmii.onion/index.php?topic=33755.msg384857#msg384857
"MDMA:
Dog went wild on this, I think it was his favourite:
1 layer: both 15 min
2 layer: 1st 15min, 2nd 1 hour
3 layers: 1st not after 5 days, 2nd after 24 hours."

Post by: cerberus1975 on April 05, 2013, 08:11 am
Just received my second order from Dutch and I have to say that he's a great vendor. The only concern I have is the packaging. Upon inspection, I could hear the rocks rattling around inside the package. It was only vacuum sealed a single time and the bag actually had some holes in it due to the friction created from the crystals. In fact, due to this, some of the powder had leaked out inside the packaging. I could actually smell it upon tearing open the package. I really like using this vendor a lot but if a sniffer dog took a whiff of this package, I believe it would have easily been discovered.

Dutch, could you please at the very least double or triple seal your bags so there is no leaking. Or in lieu of this, please use the MBBs in addition to a single vacuum seal... I really think this would be the best option and if you did it I think hands down you would be the best Dutch vendor here on the road.

Thanks though for an otherwise perfect transaction.

Title: Re: DutchTrade
Post by: Burneraccount on April 13, 2013, 04:21 pm
Someone decided to give a burner account a neg....funny.

And yes xrays can see "through" things but can only tell differences. Take ten sheets of paper put together in a  manilla shipping folder. If the pack is xrayed laying flat it will show only the sheet of paper providing they are all even and planced on top of one another.
Cut out a star now, place it in the pack. It gets xrayed and you will see the original papers, plus the new star you cut out. Now take a flat sheet of lsd....place between said papers. Providing its the same size and relative thickness, it will not be picked up.  Another way of looking at this. Say you're shiping balls of any size, if you throw rocks of mdma in there, the xray will see the outline of the ball plus the rocks. Now, if you grind the shit out of the product, pack tightly in the ball, then ship. When scanned it looks like a solid object with no variences. I know these arent the best examples but you hopefully get the point.
Neg away!

Title: Re: DutchTrade
Post by: DutchTradeCrew on April 21, 2013, 09:09 pm
Hi Guys,

First of all; we're sorry about the delay in our response but we have been offline for a while.
Also it's very unfortunate to hear that some of you, ordered on the 15th, never received their package. Please know that all orders are only confirmed AFTER the order is packed and sent out for shipping. But counting the customers who didn't receive on this date is less than 10. All we can think of is that a part of this shipment was intercepted, as we checked some tracked orders from the 15th and they did arrive.
We offer all these customers a 50% refund, as stated on our profile.

GOOD NEWS:
- Our listings will be back up on Tuesday April 23th
- We have improved our stealth and will be using MBB (Moisture Barrier Bags)
- As SR can't do anything in terms of refund after an order is already finalized, we won't request FE anymore (not for track&trace either)
- Track & Trace doesn't necessarily mean you have to sign for your package, however this depends on the country/region and your local mailman.
  Therefore a signature MAY BE REQUIRED for a track&trace package
- We'll be fully operating again starting from Tuesday, which means messages will be answered within 48 hours and orders will be packed/shipped and   
  confirmed within 24 hours.
- Tracking info will be provided immediately and together with the confirmation of your order. Please note that it will take 3-7 days before the tracking code will
  be activated by the post office
- Post order companies are CLOSED during the weekend, which means sent out orders will not be put in transit during this time nor will tracking info be
  activated or updated

Thank you all for the good reviews and your patience during our vacation! We are looking forward to doing business with you all again on TUESDAY!!

Regards,

The DutchTrade Crew

Title: Re: DutchTrade
Post by: Gusman17 on April 22, 2013, 06:07 pm
Just wanted to leave a review of DutchTrade's product. I had the pleasure of trying it on Saturday and was blown away.

Background: 220 lbs, experienced with mdma. Last mdma experience was approx. 3 months prior. Wife partook in this experience as well.

00:00 Parachuted about 160 mg. It was nice not to have to deal with powder--just too 2 decent sized rocks, weighed em up on my cheap scale and wrapped em in tp.

00:20 Can start to feel initial effects. A little discomfort (kinda felt like I had to shit) but that quickly passed. We were watching a zombie movie and were making jokes and laughing at the extreme gore.

00:45 Getting a bit more talkative and decided to turn the movie off as we weren't paying much attention to it anymore. Put on some Lemon Jelly and the milkdrop visualizer on the big screen. Heart rate increasing.

1:00 I had set my alarm for an hour after ingestion for our booster doses. I was feeling really good and honestly felt like I didn't need a booster, but I wanted to prolong the level I was on. I parachuted about 70 mg more.

1:00-4:00 These 3 hours were great. Very talkative and moving felt great. Danced with the wife for a bit. I don't know if the quality was just that good, or if my 70 mg booster was a bit too much, but I have never had the eye wiggles as much as I did with this. I couldn't focus on anything close to my face. I went through a lot of gum as well.

4:00 Definitely feeling a slight comedown, but not bad at all. It felt like I was gently descending from the clouds. Wife and I started making out and I immediately got a boner. I have tried having sex on mdma before but it didn't work out too well, but this stuff I shot right up. We had all kinds of sex for about 45 minutes (she got sore) and I found it difficult to cum. Finally I was able to cum and boy did I ever. I had a very long/full orgasm that was pretty outstanding. Not as good as sex on lsd, but pretty fucking good.

4:45 I needed a beer after that one, so we spent the rest of the night watching the visualizer and drinking beer/smoking pot. I was able to easily fall asleep about 7 hours after ingestion. The next morning I was a little groggy, but felt ok. Kinda had a burned out mdma feeling, but that really only lasted half the day. I also had a sore on the side of my tongue, no doubt from chewing my face off. Around 2:00 pm Sunday I had a large meal and that seemed to cure the hangover-like symptoms.

All in all, DutchTrade has some of the best, if not the best mdma on the road. And for the price, it can't be beat. Now that Dutch is going to be using MBB, I will definitely be getting more from them later this summer.

After a mini mental debate on whether to choose DT or Interways for my first 100 pack, I decided on DT and it's a decision that I'm incredibly Grateful for making.  I placed the order shortly before the DDOS fiasco, so naturally I was biting my nails for a few days.  But behold, in 9 days a letter from grand ol' Deutschland shows up :)  I chose the Track&Trace option, so I was expecting to have to sign and be at a greater risk for a CD.  I was greatly relieved when I went down to the RLO office and simply had to flash my card in order to get the package (I live at my college).  Our resident assistant, always eager to nab us potsmokers, unwittingly handed me enough MDMA to get our entire dorm rolling!
Ran up the stairs, down the hall, slammed the door, locked it twice, tore it open, weighed the rocks, and became overwhelmed with happiness.  I swear I haven't felt like that since I was six years old on christmas.
DTC I love you all!  Got a chunk weighing in at 64 grams! Also got a 25, a 16, and a 5.(approx. weights)  I had no idea that the extra 10% was still going on, thanks to your unexpected generosity I'll be paying it forward. There's gonna be at least a hundred people rolling for free this weekend ;)
Packaging: 5/5 didn't receive the new packs with mylar, but quadruple sealed if the stealth counts as a layer.
Shipping: 5/5 9 days, didn't have to sign for package even though I got a tracking number
Stealth: 5/5 I've familiar with this particular method, and it's never failed IME
Communication: 5/5 Always quick responses, and never irked by my admittedly bothersome inquiries.  Fluent english.
Product: 5/5 Biggest rocks I've ever laid eyes on, and IMO the quality is better than Interways.  Had a close friend compare it to his first time. Damn that feels good :)  I was taught how to wash, and may post my results later.
Price: 6/5 I love doing the thizzle dance and knowing that it only cost me $1.75 :) Selling $5 rolls will make it a snap paying back those pesky college loans for this semester. Can't thank you enough for that, debt sucks.
Overall: 6/5 I'm not using any other mdma vendor, ever again. Ever. Was about to hit post and literally just saw the update that they're gonna be gone for a few weeks, guess I'll just have to wait :)
The only complaint I can make is that I was asked to FE, but the tracking number was a big reassurance for that aspect.

i have a question about the dutchtrade mdma..i figured id ask here rather than make a new topic..

Title: Re: DutchTrade
Post by: slirp on June 01, 2013, 06:32 pm
Most of the MDMA on SR is very strong and very good but almost none of it is completely pure and without at least some sort of color.  If your friend is used to seeing beautiful clear/white crystals then he's likely seeing methylone being sold of MDMA.

Many people on the street look for the MDMA to be brown because if it is brown then it is probably legit MDMA.  The brown is probably often from leftover saffrole (a precursor) ... just a small amount of saffrole can probably make the MDMA pretty brown.  There's also been gray MDMA on SR that has been good.

Get an ecstasy ez-test (marquis) and test the other stuff your friend can get vs the stuff from SR/DutchTrade.  I would be surprised if you don't see a stronger reaction from the stuff from SR.  Using the marquis reagent on MDMA will result in purple/black.  you can probably reactions on youtube.  methylone will turn it yellow.

http://dancesafe.org/health-and-safety/adulterant-screening-kit-instructions

Title: Re: DutchTrade
Post by: mrmdma on June 02, 2013, 10:39 am
Quote from: slirp on June 01, 2013, 06:32 pm
Most of the MDMA on SR is very strong and very good but almost none of it is completely pure and without at least some sort of color.  If your friend is used to seeing beautiful clear/white crystals then he's likely seeing methylone being sold of MDMA.

Many people on the street look for the MDMA to be brown because if it is brown then it is probably legit MDMA.  The brown is probably often from leftover saffrole (a precursor) ... just a small amount of saffrole can probably make the MDMA pretty brown.  There's also been gray MDMA on SR that has been good.

Get an ecstasy ez-test (marquis) and test the other stuff your friend can get vs the stuff from SR/DutchTrade.  I would be surprised if you don't see a stronger reaction from the stuff from SR.  Using the marquis reagent on MDMA will result in purple/black.  you can probably reactions on youtube.  methylone will turn it yellow.

http://dancesafe.org/health-and-safety/adulterant-screening-kit-instructions

The colorization of MDMA is simply leftover organic compounds from the synth (yellow, brown, blackish/blueish what I have seen). The colored rocks may look like white powder though when grounded down. Nowadays I usually perform a acetone wash and IPA recrystallization simply because I want to minimize the possible effects of heavy metal residues. While the washing and recrystallization does not remove the residues completely, it sure helps and you get these beautiful almost glass like crystals.

As you said, you cannot distress enough the importance of getting an eztest kit. I know of a case where a guy I know almost died when he was sold a strong stimulant as MDMA. Good thing that he was accompanied with experienced friends who knew something was horribly wrong when he lost consciousness.

What people should know is that you can't trust a vendor for your life. There have been some incidents when a vendor has sold either knowingly or unknowingly something completely different than MDMA. The eztest is a small investment for the safety of you and your friends. People should also know that getting an eztest is not prosecutable in the US neither in EU. Test everything you put inside of you.

When you put an item in your cart you can see if it is hedged or unhedged.  If it is hedged then there's a 4% fee so even if the order is cancelled you'll get the original $ value of your order back minus 4%.  Unhedged you get the same BTC back, which has dropped more than 10% recently so you might be better off if it was hedged with the 4% fee.  I can't remember if DT hedges or not.

Title: Re: DutchTrade
Post by: DutchTradeCrew on June 09, 2013, 08:24 pm
hi Guys,

Just an update from our side:

Business is going very well. We are happy to have welcomed many new customers the past few weeks, which also means that messages and orders kept coming in like crazy. This is also the reason why it took us a little longer to confirm some orders and unfortunately had to cancel a few too. Sorry about this. Also because of the many orders, the post offices in our area ran out of tracking codes.
We are currently offline and plan to be back online after next weekend.

We see some of you posting questions about having enough in stock on our vendor page but still taking down our listings.
We have a bulk in stock, unfortunately we can't split it in "amount available per listing" on our page, because if we do split it, SR staff can automatically take down a listings once it seems out of stock and we want to be able to control this ourselves. Therefore it might happen that we take down our listings even though it seems a certain listings still has enough in stock.

we would like to reply to some of you guys posting on our forum topic:
- As most of you know: we're a professional, legit and honest vendor on the road so just to reply to "Mindblower" post: There's no reason for us to lower prices and add fake feedback! We would never do such thing. Feedback, customer rating and success rates are given by our customers, there's no way for us to control this or we would have to become a customer and buy from ourselves.
 
- Toomanydabs: As we told you in the messages: It is stated on our Vendor Page that messages will be answered within 48 hours. So if you send us like 7-8 messages in one day, (sending multiple messages is one of the reason it took us such a long time to answer/confirm last week), you can't expect us to reply in a few minutes/hours after you sent a messages.
Besides that; Please consider the 6-7 hours time difference!

- MrMdma: Many thanks for your advice in mbb suppliers and also for your reply on the forum, it's good to see that some of our customers understand certain things/delays.

Hope this reply answers your questions and we are happy to receive your orders again after next weekend!

-DTC

You didn't mention what country you're in but it isn't uncommon for tracking to take a while to show up, especially if you're tracking through USPS.  The benefit to tracking is that if the package doesn't show then you have evidence it didn't show with the tracking number.   There is always risk of loss of funds in these matters unfortunately though.

You write an "warrant letter" and sign it with an random signature. Include a trusted friends phone number for more credibility. If they decide to call him, have that friend ready on phone and ask him to tell that fake name when answering.

Usually the postal workers don't go that deep checking the backgrounds. They only need the letter as proof if someone's post get's stolen etc.

Your number 1. option will work just fine. If you can, write the warrant letter with a computer and print it, then sign it and then photocopy it again so it looks like your "friend" has sent it to you from overseas. Make it as official as possible. "I here by give permission to blahblah blah person to pick up my blah blah MDMA"...

I have ordered twice with DT and both times the product has been spectacular.  Just a quick question for anyone from the US that has ordered with the tracking option.  Do you have to sign anything when they deliver the package or not? My mail slot is big enough for their package to fit in.  Both times I have ordered I have not chosen that option because I don't want to sign for anything but with shipping taking between 15-20 business days I get really anxious  :-\  I feel if I chose tracking it would lessen the anxiety I get from waiting. But not knowing if I would have to sign to get my package would be counter productive..   

I've ordered from DTC with the tracking option as an optional shipping method, and one order requiring the tracking option.  Both packages were almost the same size and were identically.  (I'm 95% sure, but there might have be a variation.)  The order where I was not required to track was left placed in my mailbox.  The other order I had to visit my local office and give them the notice card and sign a name.  My mileage has varied and I will probably have another trip to the office soon. 

Both packages took 17-21 days to arrive.  Most of my intercontinental packages usually take 18-22 days to arrive, with the shortest time being 11 business days and the longest at 40ish.   Just be sure to check the mail everyday when you expect a delivery.

This method equipped with MBBs is one of the best out there, for orders up to 10G.

The next thing you should consider is that you would send the 5-10g MDMA orders as ground up crystal powder. Some people prefer safety over rocks and recrystallization is really easy to pull off at the customer's end. Vac seal it once for flatness, wipe with Isopropyl alcohol and then seal in MBB. Fold some paper around it and just make it look like regular business mail. This method also looks less noticeable in x-ray images.

The bulky method I think you are still using is known by customs worldwide and some countries specially screen for stuff that get's sent inside those "things".
